### Post by buzzingrobot on 2016-03-27
Someone correct me if I'm wrong, but the only viruses ClamAV checks for are Windows viruses. Do you have Windows files on the machine?  Mail, perhaps?

(The screenshot is missing.)

---

### Post by X-RED_Tech on 2016-03-27
Yes, ClamAV only checks for Windows viruses. And the ones listed in the screenshoot are all PUAs (Potentially Unwanted Applications, not Pick Up Artists ;)). Clam is famous for giving a lot of false positives - like many other antivirus - and generally is recommended to disable PUA detection.

---

### Post by alcatel1962 on 2016-03-27
